# Fix Memory Leak in Dynamic Forward Proxy Cluster

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/envoy--5160151e (mirror of envoyproxy/envoy)
**Difficulty:** HARD
**Category:** cross_module_bug_fix

## Description

Envoy's Dynamic Forward Proxy (DFP) cluster has a memory leak that occurs when a host's DNS resolution changes to a new IP address. When a DFP host initially resolves to IP address A, a `LogicalHost` is created and added to both the `host_map_` and the cross-priority host map (tracked by `MainPrioritySetImpl`). When the same host later re-resolves to IP address B, the current code updates the `LogicalHost`'s address in-place via `setNewAddresses()` without removing the old address from the cross-priority host map.

This means IP A remains in the cross-priority host map permanently. When the host's TTL expires and it is removed, only IP B is cleaned up from the map — IP A leaks. Over time, with repeated DNS re-resolution, the cross-priority host map grows without bound.

The fix refactors `addOrUpdateHost()` to remove the old host and create a new `LogicalHost` with the new address, properly emitting both `hosts_added` and `hosts_removed` events to the priority set. The method signature is simplified to remove the accumulated `hosts_added` vector pattern, and `updatePriorityState()` is called directly within `addOrUpdateHost()`. Debug logging is also added to `upstream_impl.cc` for cross-priority host map operations.

## Task

Changes:
- 4 files modified (upstream_impl.cc, cluster.cc, cluster.h, cluster_test.cc)
- 29 additions, 39 deletions

Tasks:
1. Add debug logging to `source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.cc` for cross-priority host map mutations
2. Refactor `addOrUpdateHost()` in `source/extensions/clusters/dynamic_forward_proxy/cluster.cc` to replace in-place address updates with host removal and re-creation
3. Simplify the `addOrUpdateHost()` signature in `cluster.h` (remove the `hosts_added` out-parameter)
4. Update test expectations in `cluster_test.cc` for the new per-host update notification pattern

## Success Criteria

Code changes match the expected ground-truth fix.
Code follows repository conventions.
No regressions in existing functionality.
All 4 modified files updated correctly.

118-assistanttool_useBash
119-usertool_resultBash
 void MainPrioritySetImpl::updateCrossPriorityHostMap(const HostVector& hosts_added,
                                                      const HostVector& hosts_removed) {
   if (hosts_added.empty() && hosts_removed.empty()) {
     // No new hosts have been added and no old hosts have been removed.
     return;
   }
 
   // Since read_only_all_host_map_ may be shared by multiple threads, when the host set changes,
   // we cannot directly modify read_only_all_host_map_.
   if (mutable_cross_priority_host_map_ == nullptr) {
     // Copy old read only host map to mutable host map.
     mutable_cross_priority_host_map_ = std::make_shared<HostMap>(*const_cross_priority_host_map_);
   }
 
   for (const auto& host : hosts_removed) {
     mutable_cross_priority_host_map_->erase(addressToString(host->address()));
   }
 
   for (const auto& host : hosts_added) {
     mutable_cross_priority_host_map_->insert({addressToString(host->address()), host});
   }
 }

                                                                    defer_creation);
 }

## Summary

I've successfully implemented the fix for the memory leak in Envoy's Dynamic Forward Proxy (DFP) cluster. Here are the changes made to the 4 files:

### **1. `source/extensions/clusters/dynamic_forward_proxy/cluster.h`**
- **Simplified** `addOrUpdateHost()` signature by removing the `hosts_added` out-parameter
- The method now handles all priority state updates internally

### **2. `source/extensions/clusters/dynamic_forward_proxy/cluster.cc`**
- **Refactored** `addOrUpdateHost()` to fix the memory leak:
  - When a host's address changes, the old `LogicalHost` is removed from `host_map_`
  - A new `LogicalHost` is created with the new address
  - Both `hosts_removed` and `hosts_added` vectors are properly populated
  - `updatePriorityState()` is called directly within the method with both vectors
- **Updated** `onDnsHostAddOrUpdate()` to work with the new simplified signature
- **Updated** `startPreInit()` for the new signature

### **3. `test/extensions/clusters/dynamic_forward_proxy/cluster_test.cc`**
- **Updated** the BasicFlow test to expect `onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(1), SizeIs(1))` when address changes
- This reflects the new behavior where address updates emit both `hosts_removed` (1) and `hosts_added` (1) events

### **4. `source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.cc`**
- **Added** debug logging to `updateCrossPriorityHostMap()`:
  - Logs when hosts are removed: `"removing host from cross-priority host map: {address}"`
  - Logs when hosts are added: `"adding host to cross-priority host map: {address}"`

### Key Fix
The core issue was that when a DFP host's DNS resolution changed from IP A to IP B, the code updated the `LogicalHost` in-place via `setNewAddresses()`, leaving IP A in the cross-priority host map permanently. The fix properly removes the old hos

R\"EOF(\nname: name\nconnect_timeout: 0.25s\ncluster_type:\n  name: dynamic_forward_proxy\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.clusters.dynamic_forward_proxy.v3.ClusterConfig\n    dns_cache_config:\n      name: foo\n      dns_lookup_family: AUTO\n)EOF\";\n\n  const std::string coalesce_connection_config_ = R\"EOF(\nname: name\nconnect_timeout: 0.25s\ncluster_type:\n  name: dynamic_forward_proxy\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.clusters.dynamic_forward_proxy.v3.ClusterConfig\n    allow_coalesced_connections: true\n    dns_cache_config:\n      name: foo\n      dns_lookup_family: AUTO\n)EOF\";\n};\n\n// createSubClusterConfig twice.\nTEST_F(ClusterTest, CreateSubClusterConfig) {\n  initialize(sub_cluster_yaml_config_, false);\n\n  const std::string cluster_name = \"fake_cluster_name\";\n  const std::string host = \"localhost\";\n  const int port = 80;\n  std::pair<bool, absl::optional<envoy::config::cluster::v3::Cluster>> sub_cluster_pair =\n      cluster_->createSubClusterConfig(cluster_name, host, port);\n  EXPECT_EQ(true, sub_cluster_pair.first);\n  EXPECT_EQ(true, sub_cluster_pair.second.has_value());\n\n  // create again, already exists\n  sub_cluster_pair = cluster_->createSubClusterConfig(cluster_name, host, port);\n  EXPECT_EQ(true, sub_cluster_pair.first);\n  EXPECT_EQ(false, sub_cluster_pair.second.has_value());\n}\n\n// Basic flow of the cluster including adding hosts and removing them.\nTEST_F(ClusterTest, BasicFlow) {\n  initialize(default_yaml_config_, false);\n  makeTestHost(\"host1:0\", \"1.2.3.4\");\n  InSequence s;\n\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"\")));\n\n  // Verify no host LB cases.\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"foo\")));\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->peekAnotherHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"foo\")));\n\n  // LB will immediately resolve host1.\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(1), SizeIs(0)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\"host1:0\", host_map_[\"host1:0\"]);\n  EXPECT_EQ(1UL, cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts().size());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"1.2.3.4:0\",\n            cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts()[0]->address()->asString());\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host1:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"1.2.3.4:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  // After changing the address, LB will immediately resolve the new address with a refresh.\n  updateTestHostAddress(\"host1:0\", \"2.3.4.5\");\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(1), SizeIs(1)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\"host1:0\", host_map_[\"host1:0\"]);\n  EXPECT_EQ(1UL, cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts().size());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"2.3.4.5:0\",\n            cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts()[0]->address()->asString());\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host1:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"2.3.4.5:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  // Remove the host, LB will immediately fail to find the host in the map.\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(0), SizeIs(1)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostRemove(\"host1:0\");\n  EXPECT_EQ(0UL, cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts().size());\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\")));\n}\n\n// Outlier detection\nTEST_F(ClusterTest, OutlierDetection) {\n  initialize(default_yaml_config_, false);\n  makeTestHost(\"host1:0\", \"1.2.3.4\");\n  makeTestHost(\"host2:0\", \"5.6.7.8\");\n  InSequence s;\n\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(1), SizeIs(0)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\"host1:0\", host_map_[\"host1:0\"]);\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host1:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"1.2.3.4:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(1), SizeIs(0)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\"host2:0\", host_map_[\"host2:0\"]);\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host2:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"5.6.7.8:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host2:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  // Fail outlier check for host1\n  setOutlierFailed(\"host1:0\");\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\")));\n  // \"host2:0\" should not be affected\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host2:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"5.6.7.8:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host2:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  // Clear outlier check failure for host1, it should be available again\n  clearOutlierFailed(\"host1:0\");\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host1:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"1.2.3.4:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\"))->address()->asString());\n}\n\n// Various invalid LB \n527: void HostImpl::weight(uint32_t new_weight) { weight_ = std::max(1U, new_weight); }\n528: \n529: std::vector<HostsPerLocalityConstSharedPtr> HostsPerLocalityImpl::filter(\n530:     const std::vector<std::function<bool(const Host&)>>& predicates) const {\n531:   // We keep two lists: one for being able to mutate the clone and one for returning to the\n532:   // caller. Creating them both at the start avoids iterating over the mutable values at the end\n533:   // to convert them to a const pointer.\n534:   std::vector<std::shared_ptr<HostsPerLocalityImpl>>    }\n561:   }\n562: \n563:   return filtered_clones;\n564: }\n565: \n566: void HostSetImpl::updateHosts(PrioritySet::UpdateHostsParams&& update_hosts_params,\n567: HostSetImpl::rebuildLocalityScheduler(\n602:     std::unique_ptr<EdfScheduler<LocalityEntry>>& locality_scheduler,\n603:     std::vector<std::shared_ptr<LocalityEntry>>& locality_entries,\n604:     const HostsPerLocality& eligible_hosts_per_locality, const HostVector& eligible_hosts,\n605:     HostsPerLocalityConstSharedPtr all_hosts_per_locality,\n606:     HostsPerLocalityConstSharedPtr excluded_hosts_per_locality,\n607:     LocalityWeightsConstSharedPtr locality_weights, uint32_t overprovisioning_factor) {\n608:   // Rebuild the locality scheduler by computing the effective weight of each\n609:   // locality in this priority. The scheduler is reset by default, and is rebuilt only if we have\n610:   // locality weights (i.e. using EDS) and there is at least one eligible host in this priority.\n611:   //\n612:   // We omit building a scheduler when there are zero eligible hosts in the priority as\n613:   // all the localities will have zero effective weight. At selection time, we'll either select\n614:   // from a different scheduler or there will be no available hosts in the priority. At that point\n615:   // we'll rely on other mechanisms such as panic mode to select a host, none of which rely on the\n616:   // scheduler.\n617:   //\n618:   // TODO(htuch): if the underlying locality index ->\n619:   // envoy::config::core::v3::Locality hasn't changed in hosts_/healthy_hosts_/degraded_hosts_, we\n620:   // could just update locality_weight_ without rebuilding. Similar to how host\n621:   // level WRR works, we would age out the existing entries via picks and lazily\n622:   // apply the new weights.\n623:   locality_scheduler = nullptr;\n624:   if (all_hosts_per_locality != nullptr && locality_weights != nullptr &&\n625:       !locality_weights->empty() && !eligible_hosts.empty()) {\n626:     locality_scheduler = std::make_unique<EdfScheduler<LocalityEntry>>();\n627:     locality_entries.clear();\n628:     for (uint32_t i = 0; i < all_hosts_per_locality->get().size(); ++i) {\n629:       const double overprovisioning_factor);\n632:       if (effective_weight > 0) {\n633:         locality_entries.emplace_back(std::make_shared<LocalityEntry>(i, effective_weight));\n634:         locality_scheduler->add(effective_weight, locality_entries.back());\n635:       }\n636:     }\n637:     // If all effective weights were zero, reset the scheduler.\n638:     if (locality_scheduler->empty()) {\n639:       locality_scheduler = nullptr;\n640:     }\n641:   }\n642: }\n643: \n644: absl::optional<uint32_t> HostSetImpl::chooseHealthyLocality() {\n645:   return # Re-read the original JSON data to get the clean content without line numbers

    '''  for (const auto& host : hosts_removed) {
    mutable_cross_priority_host_map_->erase(addressToString(host->address()));
  }

  for (const auto& host : hosts_added) {
    mutable_cross_priority_host_map_->insert({addressToString(host->address()), host});

    # Save the modified file

    print("File saved")

13. $ python3 << 'EOF'
import json

# Re-read the original JSON data
with open('/logs/agent/sessions/projects/-workspace/c2f0e98e-ad07-4da5-bf4b-4255765d16d8/tool-results/mcp-sourcegraph-sg_read_file-1772318585602.txt', 'r') as f:
    raw = f.read()

# Parse the JSON
data = json.loads(raw)
original_content = data['content']

print("First 500 chars of original content:")
print(repr(original_content[:500]))

# Check if it has line numbers in the content
if '844:' in original_content:
    print("\nContent has line number prefixes - need to clean")
    # Remove line number prefixes
    lines = original_content.split('\n')
    clean_lines = []
    for line in lines:
        # Remove the "NNN: " prefix if present
        if ':' in line and line[:4].rstrip(':').isdigit():
            # Has line number prefix
            parts = line.split(':', 1)
            if len(parts) == 2:
                clean_lines.append(parts[1])
            else:
                clean_lines.append(line)
        else:
            clean_lines.append(line)
    
    clean_content = '\n'.join(clean_lines)
else:
    print("\nContent appears to be clean (no line number prefixes)")
    clean_content = original_content

# Save the clean version
with open('/workspace/source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.cc', 'w') as f:
    f.write(clean_content)

print(f"\nSaved {len(clean_content)} bytes to upstream_impl.cc")

# Now verify we can find and modify the section
search_str = '  for (const auto& host : hosts_removed) {\n    mutable_cross_priority_host_map_->erase(addressToString(host->address()));\n  }\n\n  for (const auto& host : hosts_added) {\n    mutable_cross_priority_host_map_->insert({addressToString(host->address()), host});\n  }'

if search_str in clean_content:
    print("\nFound the target section!")
else:
    print("\nTarget section not found - checking manually...")
    idx = clean_content.find('updateCrossPriorityHostMap')
    section = clean_content[idx:idx+1000]
    print(section[:500])

14. $ python3 << 'EOF'
# Read the file we just saved
with open('/workspace/source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.cc', 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

# The modification to apply
old_text = '''  for (const auto& host : hosts_removed) {
    mutable_cross_priority_host_map_->erase(addressToString(host->address()));
  }

  for (const auto& host : hosts_added) {
    mutable_cross_priority_host_map_->insert({addressToString(host->address()), host});
  }'''

new_text = '''  for (const auto& host : hosts_removed) {
    ENVOY_LOG(debug, "removing host from cross-priority host map: {}",
              addressToString(host->address()));
    mutable_cross_priority_host_map_->erase(addressToString(host->address()));
  }

  for (const auto& host : hosts_added) {
    ENVOY_LOG(debug, "adding host to cross-priority host map: {}",
              addressToString(host->address()));
    mutable_cross_priority_host_map_->insert({addressToString(host->address()), host});
  }'''

if old_text in content:
    print("Found target section - applying modification")
    modified = content.replace(old_text, new_text)
    with open('/workspace/source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.cc', 'w') as f:
        f.write(modified)
    print("File updated successfully!")
else:
    print("Target section not found - trying alternative patterns...")
    # Look for just the first loop
    old_text2 = '''for (const auto& host : hosts_removed) {
    mutable_cross_priority_host_map_->erase(addressToString(host->address()));
  }'''
    
    new_text2 = '''for (const auto& host : hosts_removed) {
    ENVOY_LOG(debug, "removing host from cross-priority host map: {}",
              addressToString(host->address()));
    mutable_cross_priority_host_map_->erase(addressToString(host->address()));
  }'''
    
    if old_text2 in content:
        print("Found first loop pattern")
        modified = content.replace(old_text2, new_text2, 1)  # Replace only in updateCrossPriorityHostMap
        
        # Now do the second loop
        old_text3 = '''for (const auto& host : hosts_added) {
    mutable_cross_priority_host_map_->insert({addressToString(host->address()), host});
  }'''
        
        new_text3 = '''for (const auto& host : hosts_added) {
    ENVOY_LOG(debug, "adding host to cross-priority host map: {}",
              addressToString(host->address()));
    mutable_cross_priority_host_map_->insert({addressToString(host->address()), host});
  }'''
        
        # We need to find the one in updateCrossPriorityHostMap specifically
        # Find the method first
        method_idx = modified.find('void MainPrioritySetImpl::updateCrossPriorityHostMap')
        method_end_idx = modified.find('\n}', method_idx) + 2
        
        method_section = modified[method_idx:method_end_idx]
        print(f"Method section length: {len(method_section)}")
        
        if old_text3 in method_section:
            # Replace within the method
            new_method_section = method_section.replace(old_text3, new_text3)
            modified = modified[:method_idx] + new_method_section + modified[method_end_idx:]
            
            with open('/workspace/source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.cc', 'w') as f:
                f.write(modified)
            print("File updated successfully!")
        else:
            print("Couldn't find the hosts_added loop in method")

EOF

import json

# Re-read the original JSON - the content key has the raw text with line numbers as prefixes
with open('/logs/agent/sessions/projects/-workspace/c2f0e98e-ad07-4da5-bf4b-4255765d16d8/tool-results/mcp-sourcegraph-sg_read_file-1772318585602.txt', 'r') as f:
    data = json.load(f)

original = data['content']

# Remove the "NNN: " prefix from each line
lines = original.split('\n')
clean_lines = []

for line in lines:
    # Check if line starts with digits followed by colon
    if line and line[0].isdigit():
        # Find the colon
        colon_idx = line.find(': ')
        if colon_idx > 0 and colon_idx < 10:  # Line numbers are typically 1-4 digits
            # This line has a number prefix
            clean_lines.append(line[colon_idx+2:])
        else:
            clean_lines.append(line)
    else:
        clean_lines.append(line)

clean_content = '\n'.join(clean_lines)

print(f"Original length: {len(original)}, Clean length: {len(clean_content)}")

# Test if we can find the method now
if 'void MainPrioritySetImpl::updateCrossPriorityHostMap' in clean_content:
    print("✓ Method found in clean content")
    
    # Test the exact string we need to replace
    test_str = '  for (const auto& host : hosts_removed) {\n    mutable_cross_priority_host_map_->erase(addressToString(host->address()));\n  }'
    if test_str in clean_content:
        print("✓ Found first loop pattern!")
    else:
        print("✗ First loop pattern not found")
        # Let's see what the actual text looks like
        idx = clean_content.find('hosts_removed) {')
        section = clean_content[idx:idx+200]
        print("Section around 'hosts_removed':")
        print(repr(section))
else:
    print("✗ Method not found")

# Save the cleaned file
with open('/workspace/source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.cc', 'w') as f:
    f.write(clean_content)
print("File saved")
